<username>Basuri Bhakta<//username>< Review>
I wish someone had left an honest review like the one I am about to leave. It would have saved me from a loss of thousands of dollars worth of personal belongings. I've only had my storage unit for a month. Before I even moved in, the manager asked me to leave a review for her right while she was standing in front of me and before I even had an actual experience with the facility. Now after a month I'm able to leave an honest review. My unit was broken into despite it having an overlock from the facility. Inside my unit was everything I owned and 90% of it was stolen. It's obvious my stuff was stolen by another tenant since you need a code to enter through the only entrance. There is only a camera in the front by the gate and in the office, and there are no cameras anywhere near the units so there's no way to identify any robbers. Management told my friend that this is a common occurrence at this site yet you don't see that online. Management also did not do anything to help with the aftermath of the robbery and also took no responsibility for lack of security in the facility. I thought I could trust a big name like Public Storage to safely store my belongings in but it had only been a month and I lost almost everything I owned. Highly regret storing my stuff here. Would never recommend this place to anyone</Review>

<review>ours small and intimate! I love the quality over quantity idea. Excellent coffee! The manager suggested the Signature latte, which is lavender and vanilla.  Their syrups are all organic and homemade!  They have a guy whose only job, is to make their syrup, and his only restriction is, that he is not allowed to use high fructose corn syrup! (Which i love) The bagels are homemade too, the croissants are baked fresh everyday!  The sandwiches are hand crafted for quality!  Just great food all around! I had the acai bowl,  my friends had the egg and smoked salmon, and an off menu item (Which she loved) called the Spicy J! Soo good, the food is TOTALLY WORTH THE WAIT!  Just realize that there is one person working at all times, and food this good, should never be rushed!< /review>< Pics>

<Text>I'm absolutely impressed with the place!! How come I didn't know about them before?
I was in the area and decided to stop by for lunch. They were amazing from start to finish. Not only the food was delicious, but also the service was great!
They have varieties of everything: coffee, tea, cookies, sandwiches, macaroons, vegan, etc. The most important part is - it's organic! I got avocado toast and it was absolutely delightful. If you're looking for a cozy, affordable place to eat with great service and amazing food, I highly recommend to try them out! You won't regret! < text>
Awful beer. Asked for the 5x$10 sampler and tried one after another trying to find a decent beer but each and every one tasted disgustingly. One was too water down to the point I was hilariously grossed out. Temperature on beers were too hot, even in the winter afternoon. Next one tasted rancid and the other once had a banana aftertaste and the bad experience continued on and on. A friend of a friend suggested the place so at one point I started to suspect I was in a hidden camera or that they were playing a prank on me but it turned out it was all real. Too bad because it is a very cozy place and the guy at the bar is a nice fella. I hate to give this place a bad review, but they really need to figure out their recipes and get some help with the storage and tapping system if they wish to stay in business. I brew my own beer, so hopefully they will give some credit to this feedback.<//text>

< Review>
During Covid-19 this business did the best possible in order to make everyone comfortable with seating outside. The tables were space properly and all rules were followed to the letter. I must congratulate Mimi's chef for the best prepared eggs benedict and corned beef hash that I've ever had anywhere. Eggs benedict brilliantly done. Impeccably prepared with no detail left out. I challenge any chef to come close. As I feel I've eaten my share of eggs benedict every weekend for the last 30 years. I would say I've had my share these are by far the best.. the muffin was crispy at the bottom outer layer, yet very tender and soft center. The egg is perfectly done, the yolk center flowed slightly not hard. The corned beef was served hot with a light crispy layer. The Hollandaise was very light but the flavor was defined as decadent. A small sprinkle of green flavored spice. The meal however slightly suffered because the coffee was lukewarm. However they decided to make a fresh pot which gives them high praise. Please try this dish hopefully something this good, and well prepared cannot be an accident. bon appetit!<//Review>

< Review>
I came in alone, but I didn't have to wait long even during the lunch rush.    Before I was seated the host asked if the seating was satisfactory, a nice change from showing someone to a table and walking away.  The server was prompt and courteous with just the right amount of friendliness.  (I find it disconcerting to be called "hon" or "mama" by a server.)  She checked back often and the service was the best I've received in a long time.
I came back today and the food and service were just as good.  I don't usually write reviews but this restaurant definitely exceeded expectations and deserves 5 stars.<//Review>

< rate>
3< /rate>
< Text>
A rising star - finally seeing the menu getting a face-lift and much stronger recipes are in the house. The traditional spinach dip has given way to kale-based, the mussels are in what I'd consider almost a chowder base, and the chicken pot pie gained actual flavor.
What was always a challenge here was that the menu was adventurous, but the recipes never quite fit the bill. For example, during the last 10 years of supposed to be French Creole, the jambalaya had literally no heat or spices..  Blackened fish looked black, but had never touched cayenne in the pan.  Very strange menu engineering.
The menu is vastly simplified, keeping the perennial salad and sandwich favorites (almost...) and the bakery is still turning out muffin and bread varieties (but fewer than before, hopefully to lessen non-selling inventory.)
Service has been kicked up a notch, but is still sort of at an in-training level, really. You can tell there's some kind of re-organization going on, and it's probably a good thing if this particular chain will survive another 10 years. Things are changing daily, so sink-or-swim, I hope management stays the course, because there's a gold-mine if they can get the formula on-target here.
The on-table $20 french wines ($5/glass) are undersold, and under marketed (private label imported cellar.)  Probably happening because the staff isn't either comp'd on the sales, nor trained in what to describe about them.  This is a work-in-further-progress at the present.< /Text>
